# Communitarian flagging
character_event = {
    id = selinsectarian.1
	desc = "EVTDESC664350200"
	picture = GFX_evt_bishop
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = sectarian_light }

			religion = lugh
			religion = luwian
			religion = maher
			religion = malakbel
			religion = mandaean
			religion = mani_germanic

			religion = marcionist
			religion = melkite
			religion = mithra
			religion = mithra_christ
			religion = mithra_sol
			religion = montanist
			religion = neoplato
			religion = nestorian
			religion = norse_war
			religion = nott
			religion = nyasaye
			religion = nyau
			religion = palmyran_pagan
			religion = pelagian
			religion = saule
			religion = saura
			religion = shams
			religion = shiite
			religion = sol_christ
			religion = sol_mani
			religion = sol_sahara
			religion = sol_tsahay
			religion = solomonic_alexandros
			religion = solomonic_christ
			religion = tao
			religion = tarhunt
			religion = tengri_mani
			religion = valentinian
			religion = vidharma
			religion = voipel
			religion = waaq
			religion = waldensian
			religion = yazdanism
			religion = yazidism
			religion = yoruba
			religion = zal_mani
			# Reformed religions
			religion = amun_reformed
			religion = arab_pagan_reformed
			religion = aten_reformed
			religion = baal_monotheistic_reformed
			religion = celtic_pagan_reformed
			religion = christian_populist_reformed
			religion = cybele_reformed
			religion = ethiopian_war_reformed
			religion = graeco_roman_reformed
			religion = isis_reformed
			religion = jud_ark_reformed
			religion = judaism_reformed
			religion = mani_germanic_reformed
			religion = mani_slavic_reformed
			religion = mazdakism_reformed
			religion = muslim_aliite_reformed
			religion = priscillian_reformed
			religion = ragnarok_reformed
			religion = set_reformed
			religion = tao_reformed
			religion = tarhunt_reformed
			religion = tengri_mani_reformed
			religion = voipel_reformed
			religion = yazdanism_reformed
			religion = zor_angra_reformed
		}
	}
	        
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA664350200"
		add_trait = "sectarian_light"
	}
}

# Sectarian flagging
character_event = {
    id = selinsectarian.3
	desc = "EVTDESC664350202"
	picture = GFX_evt_bishop
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = sectarian_heavy }
		OR = {
			religion = aglibol
			religion = antinomian
			religion = aten
			religion = aztec
			religion = bogomilist
			religion = bud_mahayana
			religion = bud_vajrayana
			religion = cathar
			religion = dionysos
			religion = horus_re
			religion = hubal
			religion = illuyanka
			religion = jain
			religion = jud_ark
			religion = jud_sabaoth
			religion = jud_zion
			religion = kharijite
			religion = mand_ruha
			religion = mani
			religion = mani_ahriman
			religion = mani_slavic
			religion = mazdakism
			religion = plato_christ
			religion = plato_islam
			religion = plato_pythagorean
			religion = priscillian
			religion = qarmatian
			religion = ragnarok
			religion = set
			religion = sethian
			religion = sufi
			religion = talab
			religion = tengri_ahriman
			religion = yahyanism
			religion = zor_angra
			# Reformed religions
			religion = ahriman_reformed
			religion = illuyanka_reformed
			religion = mand_ruha_reformed
			religion = mandaean_reformed
			religion = sethian_reformed
			# Custom religions
			religion = shaytana
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA664350202"
		add_trait = "sectarian_heavy"
	}
}

# PROVINCIAL FLAG EVENTS #

## Start-Up Religions ##
# 001 Adoptionist province flagging
province_event = {
    id = 664350001
	desc = "EVTDESC664350001"
	picture = GFX_evt_bishop
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	hide_window = yes
	trigger = {
	    religion = adoptionist
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = province_adoptionist }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA664350001"
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = province_adoptionist
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}
# 001 Adoptionist flag cleansing

	picture = GFX_evt_bishop
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	hide_window = yes
	trigger = {
	    has_province_modifier = province_tengri_pagan_reformed
		NOT = { religion = tengri_pagan_reformed }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA664351R66"
		remove_province_modifier = province_tengri_pagan_reformed
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = province_conversion
			duration = 9125
		}
	}
}
